<div class="mobile-cart-icon" id="s-mobile-shopping-cart-new"></div><div class="navbar-drawer-title-container"></div></div></div><div id="navbar-drawer-mask"></div><div class="navbar-drawer strikingly-drawer bottom-border"><ul id="nav-drawer-list"><span><li><a class="navbar-drawer-item s-font-body" href="/our-approach" target="_self">Our Approach</a></li></span><span><li><div class="navbar-drawer-item s-font-body navbar-drawer-dropdown"><a><span>About us</span></a><ul><li><a class="navbar-drawer-item s-font-body" href="/vision-and-mission" target="_self">Vision and mission</a></li><li><a class="navbar-drawer-item s-font-body" href="/our-team" target="_self">Our team</a></li><li><a class="navbar-drawer-item s-font-body" href="/work-for-us" target="_self">Work for us</a></li><li><a class="navbar-drawer-item s-font-body" href="/awards" target="_self">Awards</a></li><li><a class="navbar-drawer-item s-font-body" href="/blog" target="_self">Blog</a></li></ul></div></li></span><li id="mobileLoginDropdown"></li><li id="mobileLangSwitcher"></li></ul></div><div class="mobile-actions"><ul id="mobile-action-list"></ul></div></div><div class="page-wrapper"><div id="prerendered-inline-theme-html"></div><ul class="slides s-page-30" style="display:block"><li class="slide s-section-1 s-first-visible-section css-izs5it" id="section-f_1eea48bb-888c-4d1a-8c5c-b1a91cb646cc"><div class="waypoint"></div><a class="section-anchor"></a><div>
<div class="lazyload s-no-bg s-new-text-section s-section s-text-section background-image" data-react-style="{}"><div class="container"><div class="clearfix"><div class="columns sixteen"><div class="s-title-group"><div class="s-title"><div class="s-component s-text"><h1 class=""><div class="s-component-content s-font-title"><h1><p>Privacy Policy</p></h1></div></h1></div></div><div class="s-subtitle"><div class="s-component s-text"><h4 class=""></h4></div></div></div></div></div><div class="">
<div class="s-mh s-repeatable"><div><div class="sixteen columns no-float s-repeatable-item" data-sorting-index="0"><div class="s-mhi"><div class="s-item-text-group"><div class="s-item-text"><div class="s-component s-text"><div class=""><div class="s-component-content s-font-body"><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Your privacy is important to us. It is Zensor NV's policy to respect your privacy regarding any information we may collect from you across our website, https://www.zensor.be, and other sites we own and operate.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Information we collect</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Log data</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">When you visit our website, our servers may automatically log the standard data provided by your web browser. This data is considered “non-identifying information”, as it does not personally identify you on its own. It may include your computer’s Internet Protocol (IP) address, your browser type and version, the pages you visit, the time and date of your visit, the time spent on each page, and other details.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We may also collect data about the device you are using to access our website. This data may include the device type, operating system, unique device identifiers, device settings, and geo-location data. What we collect can depend on the individual settings of your device and software. We recommend checking the policies of your device manufacturer or software provider to learn what information they make available to us.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Personal information</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We may ask for personal information, such as your:</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Name, Email</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">This data is considered “identifying information”, as it can personally identify you. We only request personal information relevant to providing you with a service, and only use it to help provide or improve this service.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">How we collect information</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We collect information by fair and lawful means, with your knowledge and consent. We also let you know why we’re collecting it and how it will be used. You are free to refuse our request for this information, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired services without it.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Use of information</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We may use a combination of identifying and non-identifying information to understand who our visitors are, how they use our services, and how we may improve their experience of our website in future. We do not disclose the specifics of this information publicly, but may share aggregated and anonymised versions of this information, for example, in website and customer usage trend reports.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We may use your personal details to contact you with updates about our website and services, along with promotional content that we believe may be of interest to you. If you wish to opt out of receiving promotional content, you can follow the “unsubscribe” instructions provided alongside any promotional correspondence from us.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Data processing and storage</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">The personal information we collect is stored and processed in Belgium, or where we or our partners, affiliates and third-party providers maintain facilities. We only transfer data within jurisdictions subject to data protection laws that reflect our commitment to protecting the privacy of our users.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We only retain personal information for as long as necessary to provide a service, or to improve our services in future. While we retain this data, we will protect it within commercially acceptable means to prevent loss and theft, as well as unauthorised access, disclosure, copying, use or modification. That said, we advise that no method of electronic transmission or storage is 100% secure, and cannot guarantee absolute data security.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">If you request your personal information be deleted, or where your personal information becomes no longer relevant to our operations, we will erase it from our system within a reasonable timeframe.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Cookies</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We use “cookies” to collect information about you and your activity across our site. A cookie is a small piece of data that our website stores on your computer, and accesses each time you visit, so we can understand how you use our site. This helps us serve you content based on preferences you have specified. Please refer to our Cookie Policy for more information.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Third-party access to information</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We use third-party services for:</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Analytics trackingUser authenticationAdvertising and promotionContent marketingEmail marketing</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">These services may access our data solely for the purpose of performing specific tasks on our behalf. We do not share any personally identifying information with them without your explicit consent. We do not give them permission to disclose or use any of our data for any other purpose.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We may, from time to time, allow limited access to our data by external consultants and agencies for the purpose of analysis and service improvement. This access is only permitted for as long as necessary to perform a specific function. We only work with external agencies whose privacy policies align with ours.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We will refuse government and law enforcement requests for data if we believe a request is too broad or unrelated to its stated purpose. However, we may cooperate if we believe the requested information is necessary and appropriate to comply with legal process, to protect our own rights and property, to protect the safety of the public and any person, to prevent a crime, or to prevent what we reasonably believe to be illegal, legally actionable, or unethical activity.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We do not otherwise share or supply personal information to third parties. We do not sell or rent your personal information to marketers or third parties.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Limits of our policy</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">This privacy policy only covers Zensor NV's own collecting and handling of data. We only work with partners, affiliates and third-party providers whose privacy policies align with ours, however we cannot accept responsibility or liability for their respective privacy practices.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Our website may link to external sites that are not operated by us. Please be aware that we have no control over the content and policies of those sites, and cannot accept responsibility or liability for their respective privacy practices.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Changes to this policy</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">At our discretion, we may change our privacy policy to reflect current acceptable practices. We will take reasonable steps to let users know about changes via our website. If you are a registered user on https://www.zensor.be, we will notify you using the contact details saved in your account. Your continued use of this site after any changes to this policy will be regarded as acceptance of our practices around privacy and personal information.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Your rights and responsibilities</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">As our user, you have the right to be informed about how your data is collected and used. You are entitled to know what data we collect about you, and how it is processed. You are entitled to correct and update any personal information about you, and to request this information be deleted. You may amend or remove your account information at any time, using the tools provided in your account control panel.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">You are entitled to restrict or object to our use of your data, while retaining the right to use your personal information for your own purposes. You have the right to opt out of data about you being used in decisions based solely on automated processing.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Feel free to contact us if you have any concerns or questions about how we handle your data and personal information.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Zensor NV Data Controller</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Maarten Durie</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">privacy@zensor.be</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">This policy is effective as of 14 May 2018.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Cookie Policy</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We use cookies to help improve your experience of https://www.zensor.be. This cookie policy is part of Zensor NV's privacy policy, and covers the use of cookies between your device and our site. We also provide basic information on third-party services we may use, who may also use cookies as part of their service, though they are not covered by our policy.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">If you don’t wish to accept cookies from us, you should instruct your browser to refuse cookies from https://www.zensor.be, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired content and services.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">What is a cookie?</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">A cookie is a small piece of data that a website stores on your device when you visit, typically containing information about the website itself, a unique identifier that allows the site to recognise your web browser when you return, additional data that serves the purpose of the cookie, and the lifespan of the cookie itself.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Cookies are used to enable certain features (eg. logging in), to track site usage (eg. analytics), to store your user settings (eg. timezone, notification preferences), and to personalise your content (eg. advertising, language).</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Cookies set by the website you are visiting are normally referred to as “first-party cookies”, and typically only track your activity on that particular site. Cookies set by other sites and companies (ie. third parties) are called “third-party cookies”, and can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Types of cookies and how we use them</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Essential cookies</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Essential cookies are crucial to your experience of a website, enabling core features like user logins, account management, shopping carts and payment processing. We use essential cookies to enable certain functions on our website.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Performance cookies</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Performance cookies are used in the tracking of how you use a website during your visit, without collecting personal information about you. Typically, this information is anonymous and aggregated with information tracked across all site users, to help companies understand visitor usage patterns, identify and diagnose problems or errors their users may encounter, and make better strategic decisions in improving their audience’s overall website experience. These cookies may be set by the website you’re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. We use performance cookies on our site.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Functionality cookies</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Functionality cookies are used in collecting information about your device and any settings you may configure on the website you’re visiting (like language and timezone settings). With this information, websites can provide you with customised, enhanced or optimised content and services. These cookies may be set by the website you’re visiting (first-party) or by third-party service. We use functionality cookies for selected features on our site.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Targeting/advertising cookies</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Targeting/advertising cookies are used in determining what promotional content is more relevant and appropriate to you and your interests. Websites may use them to deliver targeted advertising or to limit the number of times you see an advertisement. This helps companies improve the effectiveness of their campaigns and the quality of content presented to you. These cookies may be set by the website you’re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. Targeting/advertising cookies set by third-parties may be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. We use targeting/advertising cookies on our site.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Third-party cookies on our site</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We may employ third-party companies and individuals on our websites—for example, analytics providers and content partners. We grant these third parties access to selected information to perform specific tasks on our behalf. They may also set third-party cookies in order to deliver the services they are providing. Third-party cookies can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. As we have no control over third-party cookies, they are not covered by Zensor NV's cookie policy.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Our third-party privacy promise</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">We review the privacy policies of all our third-party providers before enlisting their services to ensure their practices align with ours. We will never knowingly include third-party services that compromise or violate the privacy of our users.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">How you can control or opt out of cookies</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">If you do not wish to accept cookies from us, you can instruct your browser to refuse cookies from our website. Most browsers are configured to accept cookies by default, but you can update these settings to either refuse cookies altogether, or to notify you when a website is trying to set or update a cookie.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">If you browse websites from multiple devices, you may need to update your settings on each individual device.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;">Although some cookies can be blocked with little impact on your experience of a website, blocking all cookies may mean you are unable to access certain features and content across the sites you visit.</div><div class="normalDiv" style="font-size:14px;"> </div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div>

Your privacy is important to us. It is Zensor NV's policy to respect your privacy regarding any information we may collect from you across our website, https://www.zensor.be, and other sites we own and operate.

Information we collect


  Log data

  When you visit our website, our servers may automatically log the standard data provided by your web browser. This data is considered “non-identifying information”, as it does not personally identify you on its own. It may include your computer’s Internet Protocol (IP) address, your browser type and version, the pages you visit, the time and date of your visit, the time spent on each page, and other details.

  
    We may also collect data about the device you are using to access our website. This data may include the device type, operating system, unique device identifiers, device settings, and geo-location data. What we collect can depend on the individual settings of your device and software. We recommend checking the policies of your device manufacturer or software provider to learn what information they make available to us.

  


  Personal information

  We may ask for personal information, such as your:

  
    Name, Email  

  This data is considered “identifying information”, as it can personally identify you. We only request personal information relevant to providing you with a service, and only use it to help provide or improve this service.



How we collect information

We collect information by fair and lawful means, with your knowledge and consent. We also let you know why we’re collecting it and how it will be used. You are free to refuse our request for this information, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired services without it.

Use of information

We may use a combination of identifying and non-identifying information to understand who our visitors are, how they use our services, and how we may improve their experience of our website in future. We do not disclose the specifics of this information publicly, but may share aggregated and anonymised versions of this information, for example, in website and customer usage trend reports.


  We may use your personal details to contact you with updates about our website and services, along with promotional content that we believe may be of interest to you. If you wish to opt out of receiving promotional content, you can follow the “unsubscribe” instructions provided alongside any promotional correspondence from us.


Data processing and storage

The personal information we collect is stored and processed in Belgium, or where we or our partners, affiliates and third-party providers maintain facilities. We only transfer data within jurisdictions subject to data protection laws that reflect our commitment to protecting the privacy of our users.

We only retain personal information for as long as necessary to provide a service, or to improve our services in future. While we retain this data, we will protect it within commercially acceptable means to prevent loss and theft, as well as unauthorised access, disclosure, copying, use or modification. That said, we advise that no method of electronic transmission or storage is 100% secure, and cannot guarantee absolute data security.

If you request your personal information be deleted, or where your personal information becomes no longer relevant to our operations, we will erase it from our system within a reasonable timeframe.


  Cookies

  We use “cookies” to collect information about you and your activity across our site. A cookie is a small piece of data that our website stores on your computer, and accesses each time you visit, so we can understand how you use our site. This helps us serve you content based on preferences you have specified. Please refer to our Cookie Policy for more information.



  Third-party access to information

  We use third-party services for:

  
  Analytics trackingUser authenticationAdvertising and promotionContent marketingEmail marketing  

  These services may access our data solely for the purpose of performing specific tasks on our behalf. We do not share any personally identifying information with them without your explicit consent. We do not give them permission to disclose or use any of our data for any other purpose.

  We may, from time to time, allow limited access to our data by external consultants and agencies for the purpose of analysis and service improvement. This access is only permitted for as long as necessary to perform a specific function. We only work with external agencies whose privacy policies align with ours.

  We will refuse government and law enforcement requests for data if we believe a request is too broad or unrelated to its stated purpose. However, we may cooperate if we believe the requested information is necessary and appropriate to comply with legal process, to protect our own rights and property, to protect the safety of the public and any person, to prevent a crime, or to prevent what we reasonably believe to be illegal, legally actionable, or unethical activity.

  We do not otherwise share or supply personal information to third parties. We do not sell or rent your personal information to marketers or third parties.


Limits of our policy

This privacy policy only covers Zensor NV's own collecting and handling of data. We only work with partners, affiliates and third-party providers whose privacy policies align with ours, however we cannot accept responsibility or liability for their respective privacy practices.

Our website may link to external sites that are not operated by us. Please be aware that we have no control over the content and policies of those sites, and cannot accept responsibility or liability for their respective privacy practices.

Changes to this policy

At our discretion, we may change our privacy policy to reflect current acceptable practices. We will take reasonable steps to let users know about changes via our website. If you are a registered user on https://www.zensor.be, we will notify you using the contact details saved in your account. Your continued use of this site after any changes to this policy will be regarded as acceptance of our practices around privacy and personal information.


Your rights and responsibilities

As our user, you have the right to be informed about how your data is collected and used. You are entitled to know what data we collect about you, and how it is processed. You are entitled to correct and update any personal information about you, and to request this information be deleted. You may amend or remove your account information at any time, using the tools provided in your account control panel.

You are entitled to restrict or object to our use of your data, while retaining the right to use your personal information for your own purposes. You have the right to opt out of data about you being used in decisions based solely on automated processing.

Feel free to contact us if you have any concerns or questions about how we handle your data and personal information.


  Zensor NV Data Controller

Cookie Policy

We use cookies to help improve your experience of https://www.zensor.be. This cookie policy is part of Zensor NV's privacy policy, and covers the use of cookies between your device and our site. We also provide basic information on third-party services we may use, who may also use cookies as part of their service, though they are not covered by our policy.

If you don’t wish to accept cookies from us, you should instruct your browser to refuse cookies from https://www.zensor.be, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired content and services.

What is a cookie?

A cookie is a small piece of data that a website stores on your device when you visit, typically containing information about the website itself, a unique identifier that allows the site to recognise your web browser when you return, additional data that serves the purpose of the cookie, and the lifespan of the cookie itself.

Cookies are used to enable certain features (eg. logging in), to track site usage (eg. analytics), to store your user settings (eg. timezone, notification preferences), and to personalise your content (eg. advertising, language).

Cookies set by the website you are visiting are normally referred to as “first-party cookies”, and typically only track your activity on that particular site. Cookies set by other sites and companies (ie. third parties) are called “third-party cookies”, and can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service.


Types of cookies and how we use them

	Essential cookies

	Essential cookies are crucial to your experience of a website, enabling core features like user logins, account management, shopping carts and payment processing. We use essential cookies to enable certain functions on our website.

	Performance cookies

	Performance cookies are used in the tracking of how you use a website during your visit, without collecting personal information about you. Typically, this information is anonymous and aggregated with information tracked across all site users, to help companies understand visitor usage patterns, identify and diagnose problems or errors their users may encounter, and make better strategic decisions in improving their audience’s overall website experience. These cookies may be set by the website you’re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. We use performance cookies on our site.

	Functionality cookies

	Functionality cookies are used in collecting information about your device and any settings you may configure on the website you’re visiting (like language and timezone settings). With this information, websites can provide you with customised, enhanced or optimised content and services. These cookies may be set by the website you’re visiting (first-party) or by third-party service. We use functionality cookies for selected features on our site.

	Targeting/advertising cookies

	Targeting/advertising cookies are used in determining what promotional content is more relevant and appropriate to you and your interests. Websites may use them to deliver targeted advertising or to limit the number of times you see an advertisement. This helps companies improve the effectiveness of their campaigns and the quality of content presented to you. These cookies may be set by the website you’re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. Targeting/advertising cookies set by third-parties may be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. We use targeting/advertising cookies on our site.


 

	Third-party cookies on our site

	We may employ third-party companies and individuals on our websites—for example, analytics providers and content partners. We grant these third parties access to selected information to perform specific tasks on our behalf. They may also set third-party cookies in order to deliver the services they are providing. Third-party cookies can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. As we have no control over third-party cookies, they are not covered by Zensor NV's cookie policy.

	 

		Our third-party privacy promise

		We review the privacy policies of all our third-party providers before enlisting their services to ensure their practices align with ours. We will never knowingly include third-party services that compromise or violate the privacy of our users.

	

How you can control or opt out of cookies

If you do not wish to accept cookies from us, you can instruct your browser to refuse cookies from our website. Most browsers are configured to accept cookies by default, but you can update these settings to either refuse cookies altogether, or to notify you when a website is trying to set or update a cookie.

If you browse websites from multiple devices, you may need to update your settings on each individual device.

Although some cookies can be blocked with little impact on your experience of a website, blocking all cookies may mean you are unable to access certain features and content across the sites you visit.</pre></div></div></div><script class="script-loader">(function(){var initScrollData = function(){window.cachedScrollData=null,window.ssrScrollListener=function(){window.cachedScrollData={top:window.scrollY,left:0}},window.addEventListener("scroll",window.ssrScrollListener)}; initScrollData();})()</script></div></div></div>

You are free to refuse our request for this information, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired services without it.\n\nUse of information\n\nWe may use a combination of identifying and non-identifying information to understand who our visitors are, how they use our services, and how we may improve their experience of our website in future. We do not disclose the specifics of this information publicly, but may share aggregated and anonymised versions of this information, for example, in website and customer usage trend reports.\n\n\n  We may use your personal details to contact you with updates about our website and services, along with promotional content that we believe may be of interest to you. If you wish to opt out of receiving promotional content, you can follow the \u201cunsubscribe\u201d instructions provided alongside any promotional correspondence from us.\n\n\nData processing and storage\n\nThe personal information we collect is stored and processed in Belgium, or where we or our partners, affiliates and third-party providers maintain facilities. We only transfer data within jurisdictions subject to data protection laws that reflect our commitment to protecting the privacy of our users.\n\nWe only retain personal information for as long as necessary to provide a service, or to improve our services in future. While we retain this data, we will protect it within commercially acceptable means to prevent loss and theft, as well as unauthorised access, disclosure, copying, use or modification. That said, we advise that no method of electronic transmission or storage is 100% secure, and cannot guarantee absolute data security.\n\nIf you request your personal information be deleted, or where your personal information becomes no longer relevant to our operations, we will erase it from our system within a reasonable timeframe.\n\n\n  Cookies\n\n  We use \u201ccookies\u201d to collect information about you and your activity across our site. A cookie is a small piece of data that our website stores on your computer, and accesses each time you visit, so we can understand how you use our site. This helps us serve you content based on preferences you have specified. Please refer to our Cookie Policy for more information.\n\n\n\n  Third-party access to information\n\n  We use third-party services for:\n\n  \n  Analytics trackingUser authenticationAdvertising and promotionContent marketingEmail marketing  \n\n  These services may access our data solely for the purpose of performing specific tasks on our behalf. We do not share any personally identifying information with them without your explicit consent. We do not give them permission to disclose or use any of our data for any other purpose.\n\n  We may, from time to time, allow limited access to our data by external consultants and agencies for the purpose of analysis and service improvement. This access is only permitted for as long as necessary to perform a specific function. We only work with external agencies whose privacy policies align with ours.\n\n  We will refuse government and law enforcement requests for data if we believe a request is too broad or unrelated to its stated purpose. However, we may cooperate if we believe the requested information is necessary and appropriate to comply with legal process, to protect our own rights and property, to protect the safety of the public and any person, to prevent a crime, or to prevent what we reasonably believe to be illegal, legally actionable, or unethical activity.\n\n  We do not otherwise share or supply personal information to third parties. We do not sell or rent your personal information to marketers or third parties.\n\n\nLimits of our policy\n\nThis privacy policy only covers Zensor NV's own collecting and handling of data. This cookie policy is part of Zensor NV's privacy policy, and covers the use of cookies between your device and our site. We also provide basic information on third-party services we may use, who may also use cookies as part of their service, though they are not covered by our policy.\n\nIf you don\u2019t wish to accept cookies from us, you should instruct your browser to refuse cookies from https:\/\/www.zensor.be, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired content and services.\n\nWhat is a cookie?\n\nA cookie is a small piece of data that a website stores on your device when you visit, typically containing information about the website itself, a unique identifier that allows the site to recognise your web browser when you return, additional data that serves the purpose of the cookie, and the lifespan of the cookie itself.\n\nCookies are used to enable certain features (eg. logging in), to track site usage (eg. analytics), to store your user settings (eg. timezone, notification preferences), and to personalise your content (eg. advertising, language).\n\nCookies set by the website you are visiting are normally referred to as \u201cfirst-party cookies\u201d, and typically only track your activity on that particular site. Cookies set by other sites and companies (ie. third parties) are called \u201cthird-party cookies\u201d, and can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service.\n\n\nTypes of cookies and how we use them\n\n\tEssential cookies\n\n\tEssential cookies are crucial to your experience of a website, enabling core features like user logins, account management, shopping carts and payment processing. We use essential cookies to enable certain functions on our website.\n\n\tPerformance cookies\n\n\tPerformance cookies are used in the tracking of how you use a website during your visit, without collecting personal information about you. Typically, this information is anonymous and aggregated with information tracked across all site users, to help companies understand visitor usage patterns, identify and diagnose problems or errors their users may encounter, and make better strategic decisions in improving their audience\u2019s overall website experience. These cookies may be set by the website you\u2019re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. We use performance cookies on our site.\n\n\tFunctionality cookies\n\n\tFunctionality cookies are used in collecting information about your device and any settings you may configure on the website you\u2019re visiting (like language and timezone settings). With this information, websites can provide you with customised, enhanced or optimised content and services. These cookies may be set by the website you\u2019re visiting (first-party) or by third-party service. We use functionality cookies for selected features on our site.\n\n\tTargeting\/advertising cookies\n\n\tTargeting\/advertising cookies are used in determining what promotional content is more relevant and appropriate to you and your interests. Websites may use them to deliver targeted advertising or to limit the number of times you see an advertisement. This helps companies improve the effectiveness of their campaigns and the quality of content presented to you. These cookies may be set by the website you\u2019re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. Targeting\/advertising cookies set by third-parties may be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. We use targeting\/advertising cookies on our site.\n\n\n \n\n\tThird-party cookies on our site\n\n\tWe may employ third-party companies and individuals on our websites\u2014for example, analytics providers and content partners. We grant these third parties access to selected information to perform specific tasks on our behalf. They may also set third-party cookies in order to deliver the services they are providing. Third-party cookies can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. As we have no control over third-party cookies, they are not covered by Zensor NV's cookie policy.\n\n\t \n\n\t\tOur third-party privacy promise\n\n\t\tWe review the privacy policies of all our third-party providers before enlisting their services to ensure their practices align with ours. We will never knowingly include third-party services that compromise or violate the privacy of our users.\n\n\t\n\nHow you can control or opt out of cookies\n\nIf you do not wish to accept cookies from us, you can instruct your browser to refuse cookies from our website. Most browsers are configured to accept cookies by default, but you can update these settings to either refuse cookies altogether, or to notify you when a website is trying to set or update a cookie.\n\nIf you browse websites from multiple devices, you may need to update your settings on each individual device.\n\nAlthough some cookies can be blocked with little impact on your experience You have the right to opt out of data about you being used in decisions based solely on automated processing.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eFeel free to contact us if you have any concerns or questions about how we handle your data and personal information.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eZensor NV Data Controller\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eMaarten Durie\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eprivacy@zensor.be\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eThis policy is effective as of 14 May 2018.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eCookie Policy\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eWe use cookies to help improve your experience of https:\/\/www.zensor.be. This cookie policy is part of Zensor NV's privacy policy, and covers the use of cookies between your device and our site. We also provide basic information on third-party services we may use, who may also use cookies as part of their service, though they are not covered by our policy.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eIf you don\u2019t wish to accept cookies from us, you should instruct your browser to refuse cookies from https:\/\/www.zensor.be, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired content and services.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eWhat is a cookie?\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eA cookie is a small piece of data that a website stores on your device when you visit, typically containing information about the website itself, a unique identifier that allows the site to recognise your web browser when you return, additional data that serves the purpose of the cookie, and the lifespan of the cookie itself.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eCookies are used to enable certain features (eg. logging in), to track site usage (eg. analytics), to store your user settings (eg. timezone, notification preferences), and to personalise your content (eg. advertising, language).\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eCookies set by the website you are visiting are normally referred to as \u201cfirst-party cookies\u201d, and typically only track your activity on that particular site. Cookies set by other sites and companies (ie. third parties) are called \u201cthird-party cookies\u201d, and can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eTypes of cookies and how we use them\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eEssential cookies\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eEssential cookies are crucial to your experience of a website, enabling core features like user logins, account management, shopping carts and payment processing. We use essential cookies to enable certain functions on our website.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003ePerformance cookies\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003ePerformance cookies are used in the tracking of how you use a website during your visit, without collecting personal information about you. Typically, this information is anonymous and aggregated with information tracked across all site users, to help companies understand visitor usage patterns, identify and diagnose problems or errors their users may encounter, and make better strategic decisions in improving their audience\u2019s overall website experience. These cookies may be set by the website you\u2019re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. We use performance cookies on our site.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eFunctionality cookies\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eFunctionality cookies are used in collecting information about your device and any settings you may configure on the website you\u2019re visiting (like language and timezone settings). With this information, websites can provide you with customised, enhanced or optimised content and services. These cookies may be set by the website you\u2019re visiting (first-party) or by third-party service. We use functionality cookies for selected features on our site.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eTargeting\/advertising cookies\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eTargeting\/advertising cookies are used in determining what promotional content is more relevant and appropriate to you and your interests. Websites may use them to deliver targeted advertising or to limit the number of times you see an advertisement. This helps companies improve the effectiveness of their campaigns and the quality of content presented to you. These cookies may be set by the website you\u2019re visiting (first-party) or by third-party services. Targeting\/advertising cookies set by third-parties may be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. We use targeting\/advertising cookies on our site.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eThird-party cookies on our site\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eWe may employ third-party companies and individuals on our websites\u2014for example, analytics providers and content partners. We grant these third parties access to selected information to perform specific tasks on our behalf. They may also set third-party cookies in order to deliver the services they are providing. Third-party cookies can be used to track you on other websites that use the same third-party service. As we have no control over third-party cookies, they are not covered by Zensor NV's cookie policy.\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eOur third-party privacy promise\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"normalDiv\" style=\"font-size:14px;\"\u003eWe review the privacy policies of all our third-party providers before enlisting their services to ensure their practices align with ours.
